< review>
This park brings me fond memories of when I was a kid, The main feature of the park is an old aircraft that was used in Korea. It is quite different from what it was in about 1955 when I played on it, now it is completely sanitized. Back then it was all medal and glass as it came from the Air Force when retired.
The entire park is beautifully maintained and a pleasure to visit.< /review>

<text>Nice  clean park. Generous with the playgrounds. One can handle even the big kids and then there's one for the toddlers. There's also a splash pad for all, which interestingly is not only shaded, but has 2 benches to sit while you soak. Plenty of seating throughout, with most benches providing shade at some period during the day. There's one Gazebo only. But with shading all day, BBQ grill, and 6 picnic benches underneath, I'd say it's well equipped. An added bonus for the fitness people is the exercise machines gathered in close proximity to the playground and in direct view of the toddler playground. We'll designed layout that considers the parents who want to bur some. calories while keeping an eye on their little monkeys.< /text><user>112337873431436844834<//user>< Response>

< Review>
When making an appointment for an eye exam, I was told that the exam shouldn't take more than 15-20 minutes (the soonest available appointment was right before one of my classes so I wanted to be sure I made to class in time.) The eye exam went fine but it took over an hour, which caused me to almost miss my class which was stressful but that was my bad for scheduling it right before a class. After picking out glasses and paying for them, I was told they should be ready to pick up within the next 2 weeks. Long story short, my glasses were not ready to be picked up until yesterday (almost 6 weeks after my eye exam.) Over these 6 weeks I have been the one to reach out to the office to see what the delay was. I hadn't received any call, text or email from the office to let me know that there was a delay or why there was a delay. The only reason I found out was because I called to ask. To me this is not very professional and is frustrating for me as a client and customer. I'd also like to mention that throughout this entire "delay" of my glasses, not a single staff member apologized for the inconveniently long wait for my glasses. The staff otherwise was pleasant and polite in person and on the phone, but I didn't feel as though they made an effort to ensure that I was satisfied with my experience. Coming from a background of customer experience I acknowledge that in most settings, it is expected for the business to take ownership to take ownership of any mistakes or inconveniences, even if it may be out of their control. With all of this said, my overall experience at A to Z was not very pleasant and I probably will not return or refer anyone to this location. I hope that this feedback will be taken into consideration by the staff at A to Z Eye Care.</Review>

< text>
I love Whole Foods and though this location is not my home store, it takes the icing on the cake for being a little bit different. For this location, they have $10 poke bowls, a mochi area, a ramen area, and a fast casual concept called the IRV where you can eat/drink, and have happy hour pricing from 3-6pm. Besides that everything else is about the same.  There's 24 craft brews includeing 7 local brews. If that is not enough, they have60 feet of craft brew, including local, international, and gluten free.  I saw Hopslam for $20 for a case here. Was very tempted.

Now, I can't afford everything at Whole Foods, I admit I'm more of a Costco shopper but when I want something different, something from their specialty ....like a stilton cheese to top off of my steak, I would totally come here. Say Hi to Danny if you do visit the cheese counter.

Whole Foods does catering here (that I didn't know) and can do pretty much everything except for the clown for the little ones at your party.

All stores support their local community, 5% of sales goes back into community programs. There's a celebration this Saturday from 12-4pm hosted by the Irvine Company because all the shops at the Los Olivos marketplace are going to be open. Great family event, come and check it out!<//text>

< Review>
I went to return an Amazon item, not to shop, but was curious as I hadn't been in one for years before Amazon bought it, so I walked around.
I can say the store is very clean and well stocked with item choices I hadn't seen before as well as standard products, but quite a number from other companies then Ralph's or Walmart products.  The fruits & vegetables looked fresh & appealing as did the layout in the meat, fish & deli depts.
The prices were high, though.</Review>
